(l / look-up-05 :mode imperative :polite +
      :ARG0 (y / you)
      :ARG1 (e / exchange-01
            :ARG1 (c / currency
                  :mod (c3 / country :name (n / name :op1 "us")))
            :ARG3 (c2 / currency
                  :mod (c4 / country :name (n2 / name :op1 "mexico")))))

# ::annot_utt what is the exchange rate of [currency_name : u. s. d.] to [currency_name : cdn]
# ::snt what is the exchange rate of u. s. d. to cdn
(r / rate-01
      :ARG1 (e / exchange-01
            :ARG1 (c / currency :name (n / name :op1 "u." :op2 "s." :op3 "d."))
            :ARG3 (c2 / currency :name (n2 / name :op1 "cdn")))
      :ARG2 (a / amr-unknown))

# ::annot_utt hvað býr mikið af fólki á [place_name : akureyri]
# ::snt hvað býr mikið af fólki á akureyri
(h / have-quant-91
      :ARG1 (p / person
            :ARG0-of (l / live-01
                  :location (c / city :name (n / name :op1 "akureyri"))))
      :ARG2 (a / amr-unknown))

# ::annot_utt מה הסמארטפון הכי טוב באלפיים ושבע עשרה

      :ARG1-of (h / have-degree-91
            :ARG2 (g / good-02

      :mod (a / amr-unknown))

# ::id 14516-ta-IN
# ::en_utt which is the best smartphone in two thousand and seventeen
# ::annot_utt இரண்டாயிரத்து பதினேழில் சிறந்த ஸ்மார்ட்போன் இது

      :ARG1-of (h / have-degree-91
            :ARG2 (g / good-02
                  :ARG1 p)

# ::snt хоёр мянга арван долоон оны хамгийн шилдэг ухаалаг утас юу вэ
(p / phone
      :ARG1-of (h / have-degree-91
            :ARG2 (g / good-02
                  :ARG1 p)
            :ARG3 (m / most)
            :ARG5 (p2 / phone
                  :ARG1-of (s2 / smart-06)
                  :time (d / date-entity :year 2017)))
      :mod (a / amr-unknown))

# ::snt ვინ არის ყველა დროის საუკეთესო გიტარისტი
(g / guitarist :plural +
      :ARG1-of (h / have-degree-91
            :ARG2 (g2 / great-01
                  :ARG1 g)
            :ARG3 (m / most)
            :ARG5 (g3 / guitarist
                  :time (t / time
                        :mod (a2 / all))))
      :mod (a / amr-unknown))

# ::snt อัตราแลกเปลี่ยนระหว่าง ดอลลาร์สหรัฐ กับ ยูโร คือเท่าไหร่
(r / rate-01
      :ARG1 (e / exchange-01
            :ARG1 (c / currency :name (n / name :op1 "ยูโร"))
            :ARG3 (c2 / currency :name (n2 / name :op1 "ดอลลาร์สหรัฐ")))
      :ARG2 (a / amr-unknown))

      :ARG1 (e / exchange-01
            :ARG1 (c / currency :name (n / name :op1 "avro"))
            :ARG3 (c2 / currency :name (n2 / name :op1 "a." :op2 "b." :op3 "ş." :op4 "dolları")))
      :ARG2 (a / amr-unknown))

# ::id 14209-he-IL
# ::en_utt how old was [person : elvis] when he died
# ::annot_utt בן כמה היה [person : אלביס] כשהוא נפטר
# ::snt בן כמה היה אלביס כשהוא נפטר
(a / age-01
      :ARG1 (p / person :name (n / name :op1 "אלביס"))
      :ARG2 (a2 / amr-unknown)
      :time (d / die-01
            :ARG1 p))

      :ARG2 (a / amr-unknown))

# ::annot_utt [person : พัชราภา ไชยเชื้อ] เรียนมัธยมปลายที่โรงเรียนอะไร
# ::snt พัชราภา ไชยเชื้อ เรียนมัธยมปลายที่โรงเรียนอะไร
(a3 / attend-01
      :ARG0 (p / person :name (n2 / name :op1 "พัชราภา" :op2 "ไชยเชื้อ"))
      :ARG1 (s2 / school
            :ARG1-of (h2 / high-02)
            :mod (a2 / amr-unknown)))

      :extent (a / amr-unknown))

      :ARG1 (c / city :name (n / name :op1 "san" :op2 "francisco"))
      :ARG2 (c2 / city :name (n2 / name :op1 "la"))
      :extent (a / amr-unknown))

# ::annot_utt [place_name : ملتان] کا گورنر کون ہے
# ::snt ملتان کا گورنر کون ہے
(h2 / have-org-role-91
      :ARG0 (a / amr-unknown)
      :ARG1 (s / state :name (n2 / name :op1 "ملتان"))
      :ARG2 (g / governor))

# ::id 14419-he-IL
# ::en_utt is [person : angeline] having a new movie this year
# ::annot_utt האם יש [person : לגל] סרט חדש השנה
# ::snt האם יש לגל סרט חדש השנה
(m / movie
      :ARG1-of (n / new-01)
      :mod (p / person :name (n2 / name :op1 "לגל"))
      :time (y / year
            :mod (t / this))
      :polarity (a / amr-unknown))

# ::snt ఏంజెలిన్ ఈ సంవత్సరం కొత్త సినిమాని కలిగి ఉంది
(m / movie
      :ARG1-of (n / new-01)
      :mod (p / person :name (n2 / name :op1 "ఏంజెలిన్"))
      :time (y / year
            :mod (t / this))
      :polarity (a / amr-unknown))

# ::snt በኣውሮፓ ህብረት ውስጥ ስንት ሃገራት ኣሉ
(h / have-quant-91
      :ARG1 (c / country
            :location (w / world-region :name (n / name :op1 "european" :op2 "union")))
      :ARG2 (a / amr-unknown))

# ::id 13009-he-IL
# ::en_utt can you give me the details of [place_name : indian] embassy
# ::annot_utt את יכולה לתת לי פרטים על השגרירות [place_name : ההודית]
# ::snt את יכולה לתת לי פרטים על השגרירות ההודית

      :ARG0 (y / you)
      :ARG1 (t2 / thing :plural +
            :topic (g2 / government-organization :name (n / name :op1 "indian" :op2 "embassy"))))

# ::snt כמה ארוכה החומה הסינית

      :ARG1 (w / wall :name (n / name :op1 "great" :op2 "wall" :op3 "of" :op4 "china"))
      :ARG2 (a / amr-unknown))

      :ARG1 (w / wall :name (n / name :op1 "great" :op2 "wall" :op3 "of" :op4 "china"))
      :ARG2 (a / amr-unknown))
